Pytorch教程：Linear Regression的numpy实现¶

In [43]:
import numpy as np
np.random.seed(0)
X = np.array([[1, 2], [2, 4], [3, 6], [4, 8], [6, 9]])
y = np.array([[8], [12], [16], [20], [25]])
# y = 2 * x1 + x2 + 4

w = np.random.rand(2, 1)
w
Out[43]:
array([[0.5488135 ],
       [0.71518937]])
In [44]:
b = np.random.rand(1,1)
b
Out[44]:
array([[0.60276338]])
In [45]:
iter_count = 10000
lr = 0.002
In [46]:
def forword(x):
    return np.matmul(x, w) + b
In [47]:
def loss(y, y_pred):
    return ((y - y_pred) ** 2 / 2).sum()
In [48]:
def gradient(x, y, y_pred):
    return np.matmul(x.T, y_pred - y)
In [49]:
for i in range(iter_count):
    y_pred = forword(X)
    l = loss(y, y_pred)
    print(f'iter {i}, loss {l}')
    grad_w = gradient(X, y, y_pred)
    grad_b = gradient(np.ones(y.shape), y, y_pred)
    w -= lr * grad_w
    b -= lr * grad_b
